## Build-step 33 — Phase 3: Doctor Portal + AI Decision Support

**Status:** ✅ DONE/APPROVED (2026-07-05) · **Branch:** `feat/33-doctor-portal-ai` (WORK TYPE: FEATURE) · **Spec:** `specs/33-doctor-portal-ai.md` · **Depends on:** 14, 15, 17, 18, 19, 22, 35 (gateway), 13.

**Schema/RLS/flags impact.** ONE new owned tenant table `cds_suggestions` + enum `CdsStatus` (migration `…290000`); RLS via canonical `apply_tenant_rls` (T1/T2 + WITH-CHECK + fail-closed proven in new `doctor-portal-isolation` pglite spec over 01→33). **Flags REUSED — NO catalog change, NO new permission:** the whole surface is gated `clinic.doctorPortal` (pre-existed, dependsOn `clinic.consultation`) FIRST → `@Roles(Role.DOCTOR)`; the AI panel additionally gated on `ai.clinical` (pre-existed) checked in the service. Role-gated (a DOCTOR holds ZERO RBAC permissions), like 31/32.

**Problem.** Doctors want to work outside the consultation room (review patients/history/reports, write notes + e-prescriptions, see earnings, self-schedule) AND want AI decision support — but CDS that DECIDES is unsafe + a liability. It must ASSIST; the doctor decides and signs.

**What shipped.** The doctor's remote workspace + **assist-only CDS** (Phase 3, item 3). This module IS the "33/36" clinical gateway the 17 consultation AI-assist referenced as not-yet-wired.
- **NEW `DoctorPortalModule`** (`@RequireFeature('clinic.doctorPortal')` 404 FIRST → `@Roles(Role.DOCTOR)` 403 for other staff). Every path resolves the caller's OWN `Doctor` (by `principal.userId → Doctor.userId`) and scopes to it — a doctor sees ONLY their own patients/appointments/reports/suggestions, and the `doctorId` on any write is ALWAYS the caller (never a body field → cannot write in another doctor's name). Patient scope is HARD: a patient is reachable only if they share an appointment or a prior encounter (`assertLinked` → indistinguishable 404 otherwise).
- **Endpoints:** `GET /doctor/me` (own profile), `/doctor/appointments`(?date/status), `/doctor/patients`, `/doctor/patients/:id` (profile + allergies + current meds + lab reports + prior encounters, scoped); `POST /doctor/encounters`(+`PATCH /:id`) writing notes/diagnoses (17 shape, forced identity); `POST /doctor/prescriptions` (18 shape, forced identity) — mirrors the **18 allergy contract**: proposed meds cross-checked against the patient's REAL recorded allergies (14) → an allergy conflict without `allergyOverrideReason` is REJECTED **409**, re-submit with a reason (captured); `GET /doctor/earnings` (REUSES `CommissionService.myEarnings` so the numbers **MATCH 22**); self-scheduling `GET/POST/DELETE /doctor/availability`, `GET/POST/DELETE /doctor/leave`, `GET /doctor/slots?date=` (availability − leave − booked via the SAME pure `buildDaySlots` 15 uses); **AI CDS** `POST /doctor/cds/suggest` (needs `ai.clinical` → 404 if off), `POST /doctor/cds/:id/decision`, `GET /doctor/cds`(+`/:id`, own-scoped→404).
- **CDS is ASSIST-ONLY:** the machine SUGGESTS (differentials to consider, drug-drug + drug-allergy interaction flags from the patient's REAL meds (18) + allergies (14), note summary); every suggestion is LOGGED (`cds_suggestions`, created `PENDING`); the doctor's **accept/edit/reject** is a SEPARATE, logged act (`status`+`decidedAt`+`decisionNote`). **Nothing auto-writes.** Generation routes through an injected `DoctorCdsGateway` seam via **`@mp/ai` (35)** under the exported `CDS_SYSTEM_POLICY`; until 35 wires a provider it returns the deterministic `composeCdsSuggestions` — the guaranteed **safety FLOOR**.
- **OWNS only 1 table** (`cds_suggestions`); all clinical data REUSES the existing tables through its OWN tenant-scoped repo (patient-app precedent), never importing 14/15/17/18/19; earnings REUSE `CommissionService`.
- **Pure `@mp/shared/doctor-cds`** (`suggestDifferentials`/`crossCheckMedications`/`summarizeClinicalNote`/`composeCdsSuggestions`/`cdsDisclaimer`/`CDS_SYSTEM_POLICY`/`drugClassesOf`; `DoctorCdsKind`/`CdsSuggestionStatus`/`CdsSeverity`; `DOCTOR_PORTAL_FLAG`/`AI_CLINICAL_FLAG`) — the assist-only guarantee lives here as testable code (class-based drug knowledge: penicillin/cephalosporin/sulfa/NSAID/anticoagulant/ACE/opioid/benzo/…; known dangerous class-pairs; EN+Roman-Urdu symptom cues), never left to the language model.
- **Web** EN-first (staff surface), UR-ready `/doctor` lean client island (`mp-*` classes; tabs Today/Patients/Earnings/Schedule; patient view with history/reports; write-note + e-prescription forms with the 409→override flow; **AI suggestion panel** "suggestions — you decide" with differentials/interactions/high-risk banner + Accept/Edit/Reject; earnings breakdown; availability editor + slots). Status→state gating off the API (`/doctor/me` probe: 200 ready / 401 signin / 403·404 noaccess); the AI panel degrades to a clean "not enabled" on 404. `robots:{index:false}`.

**Gate results.** typecheck **27/27** · lint **15/15** (0 warn) · build **15/15** (`/doctor` 3.48 kB / 144 kB, within the `/*` Lighthouse budget) · jest **api 712/712 (63 suites; +35)** + **db 155/155 (31 suites; +4 doctor-portal-isolation)** + i18n **19/19 parity** (EN+UR `dp*` keys) · turbo test **20/20**.

**Vertical smoke (via the e2e over the real module graph + the REAL gateway seam).** no token→401; tenant without `clinic.doctorPortal`→404; non-DOCTOR→403; DOCTOR with no linked `Doctor`→404; own profile returned; lists ONLY my appointments + patients (a colleague's leak blocked); patient view scoped + a stranger not in my care→404; encounter written in the doctor's OWN name (a spoofed body `doctorId` ignored) + audited; encounter for a stranger→404; e-prescription allergy conflict→409 then override→created; earnings via commission (own data, matches 22); self-schedule availability + slots reflect the booked 10:00 as unavailable + delete; CDS returns assist-only differentials + a drug-allergy flag from REAL records, logged PENDING (nothing auto-written) + audited, then ACCEPTED as the doctor's act; CDS ABSENT when `ai.clinical` off (404) while the rest of the portal works; another doctor cannot read my suggestion→404; empty CDS kinds→400.

**Do-NOT-break honored.** Encounter/prescription/lab/commission contracts preserved (structurally-identical rows written additively via the own repo like 31; the 18 allergy-override contract mirrored; earnings reuse `CommissionService` verbatim). CDS stays assist-only (suggest → human confirm + sign; nothing auto-writes) and goes through the 35 gateway seam. Patient-data scope is hard (own patients only). Flag-gated (portal + AI panel).

**Notes / decisions.** Chose the patient-app (31) OWN-fat-repo precedent over importing 14/15/17/18/19 services: it keeps reads+writes coherent in one store (a single fake for the e2e) and avoids split-brain module fakes, while the important invariants (allergy check before prescribing, forced doctor identity, audit) are preserved explicitly. Earnings alone REUSE `CommissionService` (one import) so the numbers match 22 exactly. The `ai.clinical` sub-gate 404s (flag-precedence: capability absent ⇒ forbidden server-side) rather than returning a disabled-200, and the web panel degrades cleanly on that 404.

## Build-step 21 — Phase 1: Billing & Cashier

**Status:** ✅ DONE/APPROVED (2026-07-04) · **Branch:** `feat/21-billing-cashier` (WORK TYPE: FEATURE) · **Spec:** `specs/21-billing-cashier.md`

**What shipped.** ONE billing surface across OPD (17), lab (19) and pharmacy (20) — the founding "cash is where money leaks" pain:
- **Unified invoice** built from an **enabled source** and adapting to the tenant's flags: `CONSULT` (`clinic.consultation`) / `LAB` + `PACKAGE` (`lab.results`) / `PHARMACY` (`pharmacy.pos`) / `OTHER` (manual line). A **disabled source is rejected (400)** — a pharmacy-only tenant can't bill a lab order (Acceptance §1). Lines are **auto-pulled read-only** from the source document (a pharmacy sale's items, a lab order's tests joined to catalog prices, a package's price) so 17/19/20 are never modified; `CONSULT` keys the fee as `amount` because the consult domain stores none. `computeInvoiceTotals` clamps the discount to `[0, subtotal]` and applies tax on the discounted base.
- **Payments** (cash/card/online/**credit=udhaar**): partial allowed → `PARTIAL` + pending balance, `paid ≥ total` → `PAID`. A **CREDIT** payment posts a **`PatientCredit` entry (14)** via the existing `PatientService.addCredit` **and** an **AR accounting event**; a credit payment with no patient → 400.
- **Refunds**: a **reason-code is required** (audited). Over a threshold the refund lands **`REQUESTED`** and only a **`billing.refund.approve`** holder can approve/reject before the money moves; at/under it clears at once. The **refundable amount subtracts already-claimed refunds** (APPROVED reduced `paid`; REQUESTED are pending claims) so an invoice can **never be over-refunded**, and `settleRefund` re-validates against the CURRENT `paid`. A **partial** refund reopens the balance (`PARTIAL`/`PAID`) so remaining money stays collectable; only a **full** refund → `REFUNDED`.
- **Cashier shift**: open (float) → collect → **close with a denomination counter → variance = counted − (float + cash in − cash out)** — the owner's **theft tripwire** (kept exact in pure math). The refund cash-out is charged to the **requesting** cashier's shift (captured at request time), not the approver's, so the variance lands on the right person.
- **End-of-day per-person report**: collections by method, refunds and variance per cashier (`collected` excludes udhaar — a receivable, not cash in hand).
- **Receipts**: thermal 80mm + A4 self-printing windows with the 07 letterhead.
- **Accounting events → 23**: each settle/refund writes ONE **idempotent balanced double-entry** `AccountingEvent` (Σdebit = Σcredit via `assertBalanced`) into an outbox `@@unique(tenant, source, sourceRefId)`; a re-emit is a no-op (`createMany skipDuplicates`). `pay` / `refund` / shift-`close` all ride **`SyncService.runIdempotent`** (Idempotency-Key) so an offline replay never double-charges / double-refunds / double-posts / double-credits.

**Data model.** NEW migration `20260704170000_billing_cashier` — 7 tables: `invoices` (money breakdown + status + shift), `invoice_items` (price snapshot), `payments` (`client_action_id @unique`), `refunds` (+`shift_id` for exact drawer attribution), `cashier_shifts`, `shift_counts`, `accounting_events` (`@@unique(tenant_id, source, source_ref_id)` outbox). Enums `InvoiceSource` / `InvoiceStatus` / `PayMethod` / `RefundStatus` / `ShiftStatus` (re-exported from `@mp/db`). Every table `apply_tenant_rls` (02); T1/T2 + WITH-CHECK + fail-closed proven in `packages/db/src/billing-isolation.spec.ts` (5 tests).

**Flags/permissions.** `billing.manage` / `billing.refund.approve` perms + the billable flags already in the catalogs — **no catalog change** (consistent with 18–20).

**Shared math.** Pure `@mp/shared/billing` (browser-safe): enum mirrors + guards, `computeInvoiceTotals` (discount clamp + tax), `invoiceLineTotal`/`invoiceSubtotal`, `invoiceStatusFor`/`balanceDue`, `refundNeedsApproval` (+`DEFAULT_REFUND_APPROVAL_THRESHOLD`), `denominationTotal`/`shiftExpectedCash`/`shiftVariance`/`canCloseShift` (the exact tripwire), and the accounting contract `buildPaymentLines`/`buildRefundLines`/`accountingSourceFor`/`cashAccountFor`/`assertBalanced` with stable `ACCOUNT_CODES` (CASH/BANK/INCOME/AR).

**API.** `BillingModule` (imports Flags/Permissions/Patients/Brand/Sync). **Present when ANY billable flag is on** — a single `@RequireFeature` can't express that OR, so each handler runs `assertModulePresent` (**404 FIRST**) then the permission (403) programmatically, mirroring 18. 3 controllers: `InvoicesController` (`/invoices` create/list/detail/receipt/pay[Idempotency-Key]/refund[Idempotency-Key]/refund/:refundId/decision[`billing.refund.approve`]), `ShiftsController` (`/shifts` open/close[Idempotency-Key]/current/:id/report), `BillingReportsController` (`/billing/reports/end-of-day`, `/billing/reports/refunds/pending`). Repo reads source docs read-only via `runWithTenant`.

**Web.** EN+UR `/billing` (`page.tsx` + `BillingClient.tsx`, `robots:noindex`): **Bill** (source-adaptive invoice form w/ live `computeInvoiceTotals` preview, recent list, pay, thermal+A4 receipt, refund), **Shift** (open float, **denomination counter** summing via `denominationTotal`, close → variance), **Report** (end-of-day per-person table + pending refund approve/reject). Optional controls gated via `/flags/me`; Idempotency-Key on pay/refund/close.

**Review + fixes.** A high-effort multi-agent review of the diff surfaced money-critical refund-path bugs, all fixed before checkpoint: (1) over-refund possible (refundable now subtracts pending/approved refunds + re-validates at settle + the refund request is now idempotent via `runIdempotent`); (2) a partial refund wrongly forced `REFUNDED` and stranded the balance (now `REFUNDED` only when fully refunded, else `invoiceStatusFor`); (3) refund cash-out mis-attributed to the approver's shift (now the requesting cashier's, captured at request time); (4) end-of-day `collected` wrongly counted udhaar (now excluded). Left by design (per spec): refunds are cash-out (the spec's variance formula says "cash refunds"), and the approval threshold uses the shared default (no per-tenant threshold store exists yet — a 41/config concern). Known limitation for 23: refunding a udhaar-paid invoice does not unwind the PatientCredit entry (refunds are method-agnostic in the spec model; AR reconciliation lands with 23).

**Gate results (all green).** typecheck 26/26 · lint 15/15 (0 warn) · build 15/15 (`/billing` route present) · jest **api 387/387 [+43]** (billing helpers 17 + e2e 26) · **db 103/103 [+5 billing-isolation]** · i18n 19/19 parity. Vertical smoke: a lab-only tenant bills a lab order and rejects a pharmacy source (400); a tenant with no billable module → 404 on invoices/shifts/reports. Perf ➖ (internal cashier tool, noindex).

**Files.** shared: `packages/shared/src/billing.ts` (+ index export). db: `schema.prisma` (7 models + 5 enums), migration `20260704170000_billing_cashier/migration.sql`, `src/index.ts` (enum re-export), `src/billing-isolation.spec.ts`. api: `apps/api/src/billing/{billing.constants,billing.dto,billing.repositories,billing.service,billing.controller,billing.module,index,__fakes__,billing.e2e.spec,billing-helpers.spec}.ts`, `app.module.ts` (wire). web: `apps/web/app/billing/{page,BillingClient}.tsx`. i18n: `packages/i18n/src/messages/{en,ur}.json` (billing/bill/shift/report keys, parity kept).

**Do-NOT-break honoured.** Sale (20), LabOrder (19), Encounter (17), PatientCredit (14), audit — all read-only from billing, untouched. The accounting-event contract is idempotent + stable by `(source, sourceRefId)`; shift variance math is exact.

## Build-step 20 — Phase 1: Pharmacy POS (Salesman→Cashier + AI Reader)

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase 1 / item 7.** Branch `feat/20-pharmacy-pos` (stacks on `feat/19-laboratory`). Depends on 18 (Medicine model + prescription routing), 14 (patient / customer + timeline), 06 (audit), 10 (offline idempotency + compensating writes), 07 (slip letterhead), 13 (UI). AI reader → 35/36 (degrades to a manual cart); batch/FEFO → 28 (stock is minimal here; sales use the 10 compensating-write hook so 28 plugs in).
- **Problem:** the pharmacy counter must let inexperienced staff sell reliably from a 20–50k medicine master: multiple salesmen build carts and **push to one cashier** who finalizes + prints an **80mm thermal slip**; stock loss must be impossible to do silently; an **AI prescription reader** turns a photo/prescription into a ready cart so untrained staff perform like experts — but **never auto-sells** (AI fills, human confirms). Plus discounts, returns, stock-out alternatives, and per-medicine profit.
- **Design decision — the money + lifecycle math is ONE pure module server+client share (`@mp/shared/pharmacy`):** `computeSaleTotals(lines, discount)` clamps the discount to `[0, subtotal]` (total never negative/over-discounted) and is what the cashier UI previews AND the server stores; `lineProfit`/`saleProfit`/`profitMargin` compute sale−cost; `canPush`(OPEN)/`canFinalize`(PUSHED)/`isStockOut`(qty≤0) are the guards; `summarizeSale` is the timeline line. Mirrors of the DB enums (`MovementTypeLit`/`CartStatusLit`/`SaleStatusLit`) keep it browser-safe. So a previewed total can never disagree with the stored one.
- **Design decision — finalize is the critical offline path, wrapped in the 10 idempotency seam:** `finalize` runs entirely inside `SyncService.runIdempotent(clientActionId)` (from the `Idempotency-Key` header) — the cart fetch + `canFinalize` guard + Sale/SaleItems create + the per-line **compensating** stock decrement + the SALE `StockMovement` + the cart→FINALIZED flip are ALL inside the seam. A replayed finalize returns the SAME sale with `replayed:true` and **no second decrement / double-sell**; guards live inside so a replay of an already-FINALIZED cart is NOT a stale 400. `Sale.clientActionId` is `@unique` as a belt-and-braces guard.
- **Design decision — stock never moves silently (06) + moves additively (10):** every decrement/return writes a signed `StockMovement` (`actorId`, `reason`, `refType/refId` → the sale) AND applies a **compensating additive write** to `Stock.qty` (`qty += delta`, upsert) — so two concurrent offline decrements both land and 28's FEFO/batches plug in without a rewrite. Returns require a reason (audited) → a positive RETURN movement + `Sale.status=RETURNED`; the money-side refund approval integrates with billing (21) — recorded now, approved there (degrades).
- **Design decision — AI reader stays assist-only + flag-gated, degrades cleanly:** `POST /pharmacy/carts/from-prescription` is behind `pharmacy.aiReader` (dependsOn `pharmacy.pos`+`ai.suite`). With a `prescriptionId` it deterministically seeds an **OPEN DRAFT** cart from the prescription's INTERNAL-dispense medicines (18) — `providerAvailable:false` until 35/36 wire the OCR; an image-only request degrades to an empty cart + a note. It **NEVER finalizes** — the salesman must review + push, the cashier finalizes. With the flag OFF the route 404s and the manual cart works fully.
- **Design decision — `/pharmacy/*` prefix avoids the existing `/medicines` surface:** 18 already owns `@Controller('medicines')` (gated `rx.write`). Rather than collide, the pharmacy medicine master lives under `/pharmacy/medicines` (fuzzy name/generic **+ exact barcode** search, extended fields, `:id/label`), keeping the module self-contained. Both modules read/write the SAME tenant-scoped `medicines` table via their own thin repos.
- **Design decision — a SALE is a PURCHASE timeline event (light view too):** added `registerPurchase`/`collectPurchase` to the patient `TimelineRegistry` (additive) and wired `PatientService.timeline` to collect purchase contributors in BOTH the light customer view AND the full medical record (a person's purchase history is the whole point of the light view). The pharmacy registers a `SALE` contributor on boot; the existing belt-and-braces filter still keeps non-purchase kinds out of the light view.
- **Data model / migration:** NEW migration `…160000_pharmacy_pos`. Extends `Medicine` additively (+`barcode`, `sale_price`, `cost_price` + a `(tenant, barcode)` index) — 18's minimal rows keep working (its `MEDICINE_SELECT` is field-scoped). SIX new tables: `barcode_labels`, `stock` (`@@unique(tenant, branch, medicine)`), `stock_movements` (the 06 §3.3 shape), `cart_handoffs` (items JSON), `sales` (`client_action_id @unique`), `sale_items`; THREE new enums `MovementType`/`CartStatus`/`SaleStatus` (re-exported from `@mp/db`). Every new table `apply_tenant_rls` (T1/T2 + WITH CHECK + fail-closed proven in `pharmacy-isolation.spec.ts`). Stock/movements/sales also carry `branch_id`.
- **Feature flags:** owns `pharmacy.pos` (module), `pharmacy.aiReader` (dependsOn `pharmacy.pos`+`ai.suite`), `pharmacy.barcodeLabels` (dependsOn `pharmacy.pos`) — ALL already in the `@mp/shared` catalog + the `pharmacy`/`clinic_pharmacy` presets, so **no catalog change**. Permissions `pharmacy.sell`/`pharmacy.cashier`/`pharmacy.stock.adjust` already present (no change).
- **API (`PharmacyModule`, 4 controllers, `@RequireFeature('pharmacy.pos')` class-wide; nav absent for Lab/Clinic-only):** `PharmacyMedicinesController` (`pharmacy.sell`) — `GET /pharmacy/medicines?q=` (name/generic/**barcode** + stock), `POST`/`PUT` (extended fields), `GET :id/alternatives` (same-generic in-stock), `POST :id/label` (method-flag `pharmacy.barcodeLabels`). `PharmacyCartsController` (`pharmacy.sell`) — `POST /pharmacy/carts`, `GET`/`GET :id`, `POST :id/items` (returns cart + `stockWarning` + alternatives on stock-out), `POST :id/items/remove`, `POST :id/{push,hold,resume}`, `POST from-prescription` (method-flag `pharmacy.aiReader`; resolves the caller's `rx.viewInternal` for privacy). `PharmacyCashierController` (`pharmacy.cashier`) — `GET /pharmacy/cashier/queue`, `POST carts/:id/finalize` (`Idempotency-Key`, compensating decrement, slip), `POST sales/:id/return` (reason-required, audited). `PharmacySalesController` (`pharmacy.cashier`) — `GET /pharmacy/sales`, `GET :id` (profit/margin), `GET :id/slip`. All mutations `@Audited`.
- **UI (`/pharmacy`, EN+UR, `robots:noindex`):** three tabs — **Sell** (salesman: search/scan → add → cart with live subtotal → Push/Hold; "Scan prescription (AI)" seed shown only when `pharmacy.aiReader`; stock-out shows alternatives inline), **Cashier** (pushed queue → finalize with a live-clamped discount preview via the shared `computeSaleTotals` → **80mm thermal slip** print window; returns), **Catalog** (Pro: medicine master add + list, self-printed **barcode label** print window shown only when `pharmacy.barcodeLabels`, recent sales with **profit/margin**). Client fetches `/flags/me` to gate the optional controls (clean off-state; the server still enforces).
- **Do-NOT-break honoured:** Medicine extended (not replaced); prescription/patient/audit untouched except the additive purchase-timeline hook; finalize rides the 10 idempotency + compensating-write seams so 28 FEFO plugs in; the `StockMovement` shape kept stable for 21/23/24/28; AI stays assist-only + flag-gated.
- **Verification gates:** typecheck **26/26**; lint **15/15** (0 warnings); turbo build **15/15** (`/pharmacy` route emitted, 4.19 kB); jest **api 344/344 (37 suites; +23 — 22 e2e wiring + 1 helpers)**, **db 98/98 (18 suites; +4 pharmacy-isolation)**, i18n **19/19** parity (EN+UR +~60 `pharm*` keys). Vertical smoke: present for `pharmacy`/`clinic_pharmacy`/`full`, absent (404) for `lab`; catalog present but `pharmacy.aiReader`/`pharmacy.barcodeLabels` 404 when off. Offline: finalize idempotent (replay = same sale, single decrement) + no-key → 400 proven. Accountability: every sale/return writes an audited `StockMovement`. Perf ➖ (internal POS tool, `robots:noindex`). Isolation: tenant + branch scoped; T1/T2 + WITH CHECK + fail-closed proven.

## Build-step 19 — Phase 1: Laboratory (Orders + Smart Reports)

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase 1 / item 6.** Branch `feat/19-laboratory` (stacks on `feat/18-eprescription`). Depends on 14 (patient record + age/gender for reference ranges + timeline), 17/18 (referral/dual-prescription → a lab order), 06 (audit), 09 (WhatsApp), 07 (report letterhead), 12 (catalog import). Manual result entry (no analyzer integration); sample is minimal here (barcode) — 27 extends chain-of-custody, 25/26 home-collection reuse it.
- **Problem:** the lab needs a full LIS — a catalog of tests with **prep instructions** + **packages**, **smart result templates** (params + units + **age/gender reference ranges** pre-built so the technician types only patient values and the system auto-flags high/low/critical), a lifecycle order→sample(barcode)→result→**pathologist approval (sign)**→branded report, plus **critical-value alerts**, **TAT**, **re-test**, **amend-with-reason**, patient/doctor portals and WhatsApp delivery.
- **Design decision — the smart template evaluator is ONE pure function server+client share:** `evaluateResults(params, enteredValues, {ageYears, sex})` (in `@mp/shared/lab`) selects the applicable reference range by the patient's age + gender (a sex-specific band beats an `ANY` band), then flags each value NORMAL/HIGH/LOW/**CRITICAL** (critical wins over high/low). The technician enters values only; the API stores the SAME evaluation the web previews instantly as they type, so a stored flag can never disagree with its inputs. TAT (`computeTatHours`) and patient age (`ageYears`) are pure too.
- **Design decision — the surface is split across the two capabilities, gated per-route:** `lab.catalog` (catalog/packages/orders/samples) and `lab.results` (result templates/entry/approval/amend/report; `dependsOn lab.catalog`). Class-level `@RequireFeature`/`@RequirePermission` set the default; result-entry & approval **override at the method** (`getAllAndOverride` → handler wins) to the tighter `lab.results` + `lab.result.enter`/`lab.result.approve`. So a catalog-only tenant can order + collect but resulting/approval 404, and a Pharmacy/Clinic-only vertical never sees the module (vertical smoke).
- **Design decision — approval is medico-legal & controlled:** a report is **deliverable only once signed** (`isDeliverable` → APPROVED/DELIVERED); approval refuses unless every ordered test is resulted (pre-sign is a non-deliverable DRAFT). Amend-after-sign **requires a reason**, appends a versioned entry to the `ReportApproval.amendments` JSON, and is audited — never a silent edit.

### Schema / migration / RLS
- **NEW migration `20260704150000_laboratory`** — 8 tables, each tenant-scoped via canonical `apply_tenant_rls()`: `lab_tests` (`@@unique([tenant,code])`, `prep_instructions`, `template_id`, DECIMAL price), `lab_packages` (`test_ids` JSONB), `result_templates` (`params` JSONB = `[{name,unit,type,ranges:[{sex,ageMin,ageMax,low,high,criticalLow,criticalHigh}]}]`), `lab_orders` (`LabStatus` lifecycle + `reported_at` for TAT + `retest_of_id`), `lab_order_tests` (records its `package_id`), `samples` (globally-unique scannable `barcode` + collect/receive timestamps + `SampleStatus`), `results` (`values` JSONB w/ the auto-flags, one per order-test, upserted), `report_approvals` (sign + `amendments` JSONB). NEW enums `LabStatus` (ORDERED→COLLECTED→RECEIVED→RESULTED→APPROVED→DELIVERED) + `SampleStatus` (PENDING/COLLECTED/RECEIVED/REJECTED), re-exported from `@mp/db`. **Permissions** `lab.order`/`lab.result.enter`/`lab.result.approve` and **flags** `lab.catalog`/`lab.results` already existed in the catalogs (LAB_TECH/PATHOLOGIST roles carry them) — **no catalog change**. T1/T2 isolation + WITH CHECK + fail-closed proven in `packages/db/src/lab-isolation.spec.ts` (pglite, real 01→19 migrations).

### What changed
- **Pure `@mp/shared/lab`** — `LabStatusLit`/`SampleStatusLit` (+ arrays + guards), `isDeliverable`, `RefRange`/`ResultParam`/`RangeSex`/`ResultFlagLit`/`PatientRangeCtx`/`EvaluatedValue`, `pickRange` (age+gender selection, sex-specific preferred), `flagValue`, `evaluateResults` (→ `{values, hasCritical, hasAbnormal}`), `computeTatHours`, `ageYears`, `summarizeLabOrder`. Reused the existing additive `TEST` `TimelineKind`.
- **API `LabModule`** (registered last in `app.module`; no global guard). Four controllers under `/lab` + `/patients`: **LabCatalogController** (`lab.catalog`/`lab.order`) — `GET/POST /lab/tests`, `PUT /lab/tests/:id`, `GET/POST /lab/packages`; **LabTemplatesController** (`lab.results`/`lab.result.enter`) — `GET/POST /lab/result-templates`; **LabOrdersController** — `POST /lab/orders` (validates patient 14, expands packages, best-effort prep WhatsApp), `GET /lab/orders?status=&patientId=`, `GET /lab/orders/:id`, `POST /lab/orders/:id/collect` (generates a `LAB-…` barcode → COLLECTED), `POST /lab/samples/receive` (scan → RECEIVED), `POST /lab/orders/:id/retest` (links `retestOfId`), method-overridden `POST /lab/orders/:id/results` (evaluate vs template + patient age/gender → auto-flag, → RESULTED when all done, `criticalAlert`), `POST /lab/orders/:id/approve` (sign → APPROVED + `reportedAt` + WhatsApp `lab.report.ready`, degrades), `POST /lab/orders/:id/amend` (reason required, versioned, audited), `GET /lab/orders/:id/report` (branded 07 letterhead payload, `draft` when unsigned); **PatientLabController** — `GET /patients/:id/lab-orders` (portal list). All mutations `@Audited`. Prisma Decimal↔number normalised at the repo seam.
- **Timeline + import wiring** — `LabModule.onModuleInit` registers a MEDICAL `TimelineRegistry` contributor → a `TEST` event per order (`summarizeLabOrder`, medical view only), and registers the **lab-test catalog importer** (`labTestImporter`, idempotent by `code`) with the 12 `ImportRegistry` (`GET /import/lab_test/template` etc.).
- **Web EN+UR `/lab`** — server page frames a client island (`robots:noindex`): access probe, three tabs — **Worklist** (orders list → open an order → collect/receive a barcoded sample → per-test result entry with the params/units/ranges pre-filled and **live flags** via the shared `evaluateResults` + fetched patient age/gender → pathologist Approve & sign → Amend-with-reason → **Print branded report** window (07 letterhead, per-test values + reference + flags + amendments + TAT + sign) → Re-test), **New order** (patient/doctor ids + catalog search + selected tests → create), **Catalog** (add a test + list). 69 new i18n keys EN↔UR (parity).

### Verification gates
- **typecheck** 26/26 · **lint** 15/15 · **turbo build** 15/15 (web `/lab` route emitted).
- **jest api 321/321** (35 suites; **+25**: `lab-helpers.spec.ts` 11 — vocab/deliverable, ageYears, pickRange age+gender, flagValue NORMAL/HIGH/LOW/CRITICAL, evaluateResults, TAT, summary; `lab.e2e.spec.ts` 14 — 401, clinic-only 404 vertical smoke, catalog-only 404 on resulting, `lab.order` 403 + `lab.result.enter` 403, catalog+dup-code 409+packages, prep-at-booking, package expansion, smart-template auto-flag by age+gender + critical alert, sample collect→receive+second-collect 409+re-test, pre-sign draft + approve gating + `lab.result.approve` 403 + TAT + report + amend-needs-reason + audit, catalog import template, portal list + timeline TEST event). **jest db 94/94** (17 suites; **+4** lab-isolation). **i18n 19/19** parity. All other package suites unaffected.
- **Isolation:** all 8 tables tenant-scoped; T1/T2 + WITH CHECK + fail-closed proven. **Vertical smoke:** module 404s for Pharmacy/Clinic-only (no `lab.catalog`); resulting 404s when `lab.results` off. **Performance ➖** (internal LIS tool, `robots:noindex`, no public surface).
- **Do-NOT-break honoured:** patient (14, age/gender ranges), referral (17/18), audit, notifications, 07 letterhead untouched except additively. `Sample` shape left minimal for 27 to extend + 25/26 to reuse; approval/amend kept controlled (sign-gated, reason-required, audited).

## Build-step 16 — Phase 1: Vitals Station (Nurse)

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase 1 / item 3.** Branch `feat/16-vitals-station` (stacks on `feat/15-appointment-token`). Depends on 14 (patient record + timeline), 15 (appointment/token — the sheet header), 10 (offline core / idempotency seam), 13 (UI/i18n). **Critical offline path.**
- **Problem:** before the doctor, a nurse records vitals on a printed A4. Two habits must BOTH be supported and neither can be forced to change: (a) type into the app then print a filled sheet, (b) print a blank header sheet and write by pen (then type it, or photo→AI read it later). AI photo-read is deferred to build-step 35; until then the photo path yields an empty draft the nurse types over.
- **Design decision — one table, every value optional, BMI authoritative on the server:** a nurse records what the visit needs (not a fixed panel), so every measurement column is nullable. The client may send weight/height but the server ALWAYS recomputes `bmi` from them (`computeBmi`, the ONE formula shared with the web's live indicator) so a stored BMI can never disagree with its inputs. Saving rides the offline idempotency seam exactly like a token (required `Idempotency-Key` → `SyncService.runIdempotent`, plus a P2002 backstop on the unique `client_action_id`) so a reading queued offline and replayed on reconnect returns the SAME row, never a duplicate.
- **Design decision — a decoupled `TimelineRegistry` instead of patients→vitals coupling:** the patient timeline (14) must show a reading, but the patients module must not import a downstream clinical module. NEW `TimelineRegistry` (mirrors the `ImportRegistry` pattern) is provided + exported by PatientsModule; VitalsModule registers a MEDICAL contributor on boot. Contributors flow IN (no cycle) and are collected ONLY when `customers.medicalRecord` is on, so the light customer view stays purchase-only automatically. This is the seam 17/19/20 reuse.

### Schema / migration / RLS
- **NEW migration `20260704120000_vitals_station`** — 1 table `vitals`, tenant-scoped via canonical `apply_tenant_rls()` + `branch_id`: `patient_id` (+ optional `appointment_id`/`encounter_id` — encounter reserved for 17), the reading columns (`bp_sys`/`bp_dia`/`pulse`/`spo2` INT; `temp_c`/`weight_kg`/`height_cm`/`bmi`/`blood_sugar` DECIMAL; `sugar_type` TEXT), `captured_by`/`captured_at`, `source` (`VitalsSource` enum TYPED/HANDWRITTEN_PHOTO/IMPORTED, default TYPED), and UNIQUE `client_action_id` for offline idempotency. Indexes `(tenant, patient)` + `(tenant, appointment)`. NEW enum `VitalsSource` re-exported from `@mp/db`. T1/T2 isolation + WITH CHECK + fail-closed proven in `packages/db/src/vitals-isolation.spec.ts` (pglite, real 01→16 migrations).

### What changed
- **Pure `@mp/shared/vitals`** — `computeBmi(weightKg, heightCm)` (→ 1 dp, null unless both positive), `summarizeVitals` (compact timeline/print line, derives BMI, never trusts input), `hasAnyVital`, `SUGAR_TYPES`/`isSugarType` (FASTING/RANDOM/PP/HBA1C), `VitalsValues`/`SugarTypeLit`/`VitalsSourceLit`. Added `VITALS` to the additive `TimelineKind` union (medical-only — not in `PURCHASE_TIMELINE_KINDS`).
- **API `VitalsModule`** (registered after Sync/Patients/Appointments in `app.module`; no global guard). Whole controller `@RequireFeature('clinic.consultation')` (already in catalog + clinic presets — **404s when off** = vertical smoke) + `@RequirePermission('vitals.enter')` (already in catalog; NURSE/DOCTOR carry it, RECEPTION/ADMIN do not). Endpoints: `POST /vitals` (`@Audited('vitals.record')`, required `Idempotency-Key` → offline-idempotent, BMI recomputed); `GET /vitals?patientId=&appointmentId=` (newest first); `GET /vitals/sheet?appointmentId=&patientId=&blank=` (composes the patient/token header from PatientService + AppointmentsService — added public `detailAppointment` + `tokenNumberForAppointment` accessors to AppointmentsService — and pre-prints the latest reading unless `blank`); `POST /vitals/from-photo` (`@Audited`) → a DRAFT (`aiAvailable:false`, empty until 35) the nurse confirms — **no silent commit**. Repo converts Prisma Decimal↔number at the seam.
- **Patient timeline wiring** — `TimelineRegistry` provided+exported by PatientsModule; `PatientService.timeline` appends `registry.collectMedical(...)` inside the medical branch (failures isolated per contributor). VitalsModule.`onModuleInit` registers `timelineEvents` → a `VITALS` event (`"Vitals recorded — BP …"`).
- **Web EN+UR `/vitals`** — server page frames a client island: access probe (`GET /vitals?patientId=__probe__`), patient/appointment id inputs (prefill from `?patientId=`/`?appointmentId=`), a big number-input grid with a **live BMI** as the nurse types, Save (online → `idempotency-key`; offline → outbox `enqueue`, never double-saves), **Print filled / Print blank** (fetches the sheet JSON, opens a self-contained A4 print window with the patient/token header + filled values or empty write-by-pen boxes, RTL-aware), and a recent-readings history. New `.mp-vitals-*` styles; 42 new i18n keys EN↔UR (parity).

### Verification gates
- **typecheck** 26/26 · **lint** 15/15 · **turbo build** 15/15 (web `/vitals` route emitted).
- **jest api 247/247** (29 suites; **+20**: `vitals-helpers.spec.ts` 8 + `vitals.e2e.spec.ts` 12 — flag 404 vertical smoke, `vitals.enter` 403, BMI auto-compute + offline-idempotent replay, missing-key 400, out-of-range 400, filled + blank sheet with header/token, photo→draft no-commit, timeline VITALS event, audit). **jest db 82/82** (14 suites; **+3** vitals-isolation). **i18n 19/19** parity. shared/ui/import/offline/consent/notifications/patients/appointments suites unaffected.
- **Isolation:** tenant-scoped; T1/T2 + WITH CHECK + fail-closed proven. **Offline:** replay returns the same row (idempotency seam + P2002 backstop). **Vertical smoke:** whole surface 404s when `clinic.consultation` off.
- **Do-NOT-break honoured:** patient/appointment/timeline/offline-idempotency/flag-gate untouched except additively (new `TimelineRegistry`, new public appointment accessors, new `VITALS` timeline kind). Vitals row shape is additive — stable for the consultation (17) to read.

## Build-step 15 — Phase 1: Appointment & Token (paper-first)

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase 1 / item 2.** Branch `feat/15-appointment-token` (stacks on `feat/14-patient-management`). Depends on 14 (patient), 10 (offline core / idempotency seam), 09 (notifications), 13 (UI/i18n).
- **Problem:** the clinic runs on paper; aged patients don't self-book; the compounder is often too busy to register fully; staff reconcile a paper register at day's end. A system fighting this is abandoned. Design **for** paper: one-tap offline tokens, full registration optional, end-of-day photo→(AI later) register import with a human verify.
- **Design decision — a Token creates a WALK_IN Appointment + a numbered Token atomically:** the queue is built from active appointments with their token numbers attached; booked appointments (source BOOKED) join the same queue; register-import commits create appointments+tokens with source REGISTER_IMPORT. Token numbering is **sequential per doctor/branch/day** via a plaintext `day_key` + a tenant-scoped unique index `(tenant, doctor, branch, day_key, number)` so numbering never collides (and co-exists across tenants — proven in the isolation test).

### Schema / migration / RLS
- **NEW migration `20260704110000_appointment_token`** — 6 tables, all tenant-scoped via canonical `apply_tenant_rls()` + `branch_id` where location-scoped: `doctors` (slotMinutes/comfortLevel/optional user link), `doctor_availability` (weekly dayOfWeek + minutes-of-day windows), `doctor_leave` (dated ranges), `appointments` (`ApptStatus` lifecycle + `ApptSource`), `tokens` (`number` + `day_key` + UNIQUE `client_action_id` for offline idempotency; unique `(tenant, doctor, branch, day_key, number)`), `register_imports` (`imageKeys` JSON + `RegImportStatus` UPLOADED→PARSED→VERIFIED→IMPORTED + `draft` JSON). NEW enums `ApptStatus`/`ApptSource`/`RegImportStatus` re-exported from `@mp/db`. T1/T2 isolation + WITH CHECK + fail-closed + no-cross-tenant-numbering proven in `packages/db/src/appointment-isolation.spec.ts` (pglite, real 01→15 migrations).
- **No new feature flag** — `clinic.appointments` already in the catalog (`@mp/shared/flags`) and in the `clinic`/`clinic_pharmacy`/`full` presets. **No new permission** — `appointments.manage` already in the catalog (granted to ADMIN/MANAGER/DOCTOR/RECEPTION/CALL_CENTER). The WHOLE controller is `@RequireFeature('clinic.appointments')` + `@RequirePermission('appointments.manage')` at the class level (flag FIRST → 404 when off, then permission → 403).

### What changed
- **Pure `@mp/shared/appointments`** (browser-safe, no node imports): `dayKeyOf` (UTC day bucket the server + offline client agree on), `nextTokenNumber` (max+1, gap-free), `buildDaySlots` (availability − leave − booked, de-duped, minute⇄`HH:MM` `minutesToLabel`/`labelToMinutes`), the appointment lifecycle state machine (`APPT_TRANSITIONS`/`canTransitionAppt`/`isTerminalAppt`), and the register-import draft contract (`RegisterDraftRow`/`isCommittableDraftRow`/`committableRows`).
- **API `AppointmentsModule`** (imports `SyncModule`): `POST /appointments/tokens` — one-tap walk-in, **CRITICAL OFFLINE PATH** riding `SyncService.runIdempotent(clientActionId)` (required `Idempotency-Key` header) so a replayed token returns the SAME number without double-issuing (a P2002 backstop on the unique index catches the save-race). Doctor CRUD; availability/leave CRUD; `GET /appointments/doctors/:id/slots?date=` (availability − leave − booked); `POST /appointments` (book, source BOOKED) + `PATCH /appointments/:id` (reschedule/cancel/status/no-show, state-machine-validated → 400 on illegal transition); `GET /appointments/queue` + `GET /appointments/display` (per-doctor now-serving + up-next). Register import: `POST /register-imports` (photos→UPLOADED) → `POST /:id/parse` (empty draft until AI 35; PARSED) → `PATCH /:id/draft` (human-verified rows; VERIFIED) → `POST /:id/import` (commit; **must be VERIFIED first**, incomplete rows skipped not guessed → 400 before verify; never auto-commits). All mutations `@Audited`. Injectable `APPT_CLOCK` for deterministic `day_key`/slots in tests.
- **Web EN+UR `/appointments`** — flag/permission-aware island (404/403 → clean no-access): offline badge (from `useSyncStatus`), compounder giant one-tap **New Token** (online → token #; network-down → outbox `enqueue` so it syncs, never double-issues), live **Queue** with Start/Done/No-show taps, **Doctors** tab (add doctor + per-doctor availability/leave via time inputs), full-screen-ish **Display** board, and the human-gated **Register import** wizard (upload keys → parse → verify rows → import). New `mp-appt-*` CSS.
- **i18n:** ~60 new `appt*` keys in EN+UR (`@mp/i18n` catalogs), parity gate green.

### Verification gates (all green)
- typecheck **26/26**, lint **15/15**, turbo build **15/15** (`/appointments` route compiled).
- jest: **api 227/227** (27 suites; **+21** — 13 appointment e2e over the real guard graph [flag-off 404 vertical smoke, permission 403, idempotent replay, sequential/per-doctor numbering, slots=avail−leave−booked, lifecycle + illegal-transition 400, queue+display, register-import human-gate + skip-incomplete + audited] + 8 pure-helper unit) · **db 79/79** (13 suites; **+6** `appointment-isolation`: per-tenant doctors/appointments/tokens, no-cross-tenant numbering collision, WITH CHECK ×2, fail-closed) · i18n **19/19** incl. EN↔UR parity · ui/import/offline/consent/notifications/patients unaffected.
- **Flag / vertical smoke:** `clinic.appointments` OFF (pharmacy/lab-only) → every route 404s, module absent from nav (proven in e2e). **Offline self-check:** token idempotency proven (replayed clientActionId → same number, exactly one token for three POSTs).

### Notes / manual-run caveats
- Register-import AI parse returns an EMPTY draft until the AI gateway (35) lands (staff fill rows manually); today `imageKeys` are client-provided photo keys — multipart upload + R2 object store = `[DECIDE AT BUILD]`.
- Token creation rides `SyncService.runIdempotent` (durable dedup via `sync_idempotency`) AND stores `client_action_id` on the token (unique) as a domain backstop; the web outbox path mints its own key on true network failure only (fetch never reached the server), so it cannot double with a partially-succeeded online POST.
- `prisma migrate deploy` / full `deploy.sh` need a live Postgres 16 + server; not runnable in this sandbox. Migration validated under pglite (isolation test runs the real 01→15 SQL) and `prisma generate` ✓.

## Build-step 14 — Phase 1: Patient / Customer Management

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase 1 / item 1.** Branch `feat/14-patient-management` (stacks on `feat/13-ui-foundation`). Depends on 02 (RLS/runWithTenant), 04 (permissions), 05 (flags), 06 (audit), 08 (i18n), 09 (notification prefs), 12 (import engine).
- **Problem:** every vertical needs a person record, but a pharmacy-only tenant wants a light "customer" (name+phone+udhaar+purchase history) while a clinic/full tenant needs the full medical record. Pakistani clinics identify by phone (families share one number; aged patients may have none); udhaar must never silently vanish; CNIC is sensitive PII.
- **Design decision — ONE model, flag-driven VIEW:** identical data model; the `customers.medicalRecord` flag decides which fields/tabs render AND which endpoints are exposed. A pharmacy that later adds a clinic needs NO migration — just flip the flag.

### Schema / migration / RLS
- **NEW migration `20260704100000_patient_management`** — 7 tables, all tenant-scoped via canonical `apply_tenant_rls()`:
  - `patients` — phone-primary (NULLABLE: aged patients / shared family phone → `guardian_id` link), CNIC stored **AES-256-GCM-encrypted** in `cnic` with only `cnic_last4` kept plaintext for search, `gender`/`dob`/`address`/`service_area`/`status` (ACTIVE/INACTIVE/DECEASED), `@@unique(tenant,phone)`.
  - `patient_relations` (directed family/guardian links), `patient_tags`, `patient_allergies` (MEDICAL-record field, severity LOW/MED/HIGH), `patient_credits` (udhaar ledger, `Decimal(12,2)`, `settled_at`/`settled_by`), `patient_notes`, `notification_prefs` (per-channel consent, `@@unique(patient)`).
  - NEW enums `Gender`/`PatientStatus`/`Severity`/`RelationType` (re-exported from `@mp/db`).
  - **pg_trgm** extension + GIN trigram indexes (name/phone/cnic_last4) created **DEFENSIVELY** inside a `DO … EXCEPTION WHEN OTHERS` block → no-ops under the pglite RLS test (which lacks pg_trgm); search falls back to a plain, correct ILIKE. Proven pglite-safe before commit.
  - Two model additions BEYOND the spec's 6-model list, each acceptance-driven & additive: `cnic_last4` (required to reconcile §3 CNIC-last4 search with §4 encryption) and `patient_notes` (backs §3.2/§3.3 Notes tab/endpoint).
- **Isolation:** NEW `packages/db/src/patient-isolation.spec.ts` — real 01→14 migrations in pglite, proves T1/T2 scoping on `patients` + `patient_credits`, WITH CHECK blocks cross-tenant writes, encrypted CNIC never bleeds, zero rows with no context (6/6).

### Feature-flag / permission impact
- **Owns/respects flag `customers.medicalRecord`** (existing in catalog): OFF → light customer (allergy CRUD + medical timeline hidden); ON → full record. Allergy routes carry `@RequireFeature('customers.medicalRecord')` → **404 when off** (flag FIRST, then permission).
- Permissions (all pre-existing in `@mp/shared`): `patients.view`/`edit`/`merge`/`notes`/`cnic.reveal`. No new keys.
- **NEW config `CNIC_ENCRYPTION_KEY`** (zod `.min(32)`, dev fallback rejected in production via superRefine). `fakeConfig()` extended with it.

### What changed
- **Pure `@mp/shared/patients.ts`** (browser-safe, no node deps): `maskCnic`/`cnicLast4`/`normalizeCnic`/`normalizePhone`, `creditBalance` (Σ unsettled → feeds accounts 23), `TimelineEvent`+`TimelineKind`+`sortTimeline`+`isPurchaseEvent`+`PURCHASE_TIMELINE_KINDS`.
- **API-only `apps/api/src/patients/cnic-cipher.ts`** — `CnicCipher` (AES-256-GCM, SHA-256-derived 32-byte key from `CNIC_KEY` DI token, `v1:iv:tag:data` blob, tamper-detecting; `prepare()` → {cipher,last4}). Kept out of `@mp/shared` so `node:crypto` never bundles into the browser.
- **`PatientsModule`** (repo seam + `CnicCipher` + `FlagService`): `GET /patients` fuzzy (ILIKE name/phone/cnic-last4, paginated), `POST/PATCH /patients` (phone uniqueness enforced → "link as family" 400; guardian existence checked), `POST /patients/:id/cnic/reveal` (`patients.cnic.reveal` + `@Audited`, full value returned but MASKED in the audit summary), family/relations + dependents + guardian, tags CRUD, allergies CRUD (flag-gated + severity-ranked `allergyWarnings` hook for 18/20), credit add/settle (returns balance), notes (`patients.notes`), notification prefs (honoured by 09), `merge` (moves credit/allergies/notes/tags/relations/dependents to target → source INACTIVE, `@Audited`), `timeline` (flag-shaped: REGISTERED+CREDIT purchase-only when off; +ALLERGY/NOTE when on).
- **Registers a patient importer** with the 12 `ImportRegistry` on boot (`onModuleInit`): natural key = phone (idempotent — re-import updates, never duplicates), CNIC encrypted at `upsertChunk`, export never emits full CNIC (masked last-4 only). Wired into `app.module` after Flags+Import.
- **Web EN+UR `/patients`** (`.mp-*` design-token convention, RTL): quick-add (phone-first), fuzzy search list, flag-aware `ModuleTabs` (Basic · Timeline · [Allergies] · Credit · [Notes] · Family — medical tabs only when `medicalRecordEnabled`), masked CNIC + audited reveal button, udhaar ledger add/settle, allergy severity picker. 61 NEW i18n keys EN+UR (`patients*`), parity green.

### Verification gates
- **typecheck 26/26 · lint 15/15 · build 15/15** (turbo). `/patients` route 3.13 kB / 118 kB first-load — within perf budget (cf. /ui 282 kB).
- **jest:** api **206/206** (25 suites; +31 = 14 patient e2e covering auth/permission/flag-ON+OFF/family/fuzzy/CNIC-encrypt+mask+reveal-audit/udhaar/tags/status/prefs/merge/idempotent-import + 6 CnicCipher unit + 11 patient-helper unit), db **73/73** (12 suites; +6 patient-isolation), i18n **19/19** incl. EN↔UR parity, ui 38/38, import 18/18, notifications 18/18, offline 29/29, consent 18/18.
- **Flag/vertical smoke:** proven in e2e — flag OFF (pharmacy) → allergy endpoints 404, timeline purchase-only, `medicalRecordEnabled:false`; flag ON (clinic/full) → allergies + medical timeline. Same data, no migration.
- **Isolation:** T1/T2 proven (pglite); CNIC stored ciphertext (`v1:` prefix, never plaintext) and never logged (audit summary masks it). **White-label:** untouched (brand tokens drive the UI).
- **Launch note:** JSON-body CNIC + in-process import today; CNIC-key rotation / KMS + multipart upload = `[DECIDE AT BUILD]`.

## Build-step 13 — Foundation: UI Design System + Performance Foundation

**Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase:** Foundation / item 13. **Branch:** `feat/13-ui-foundation` (stacked on `feat/12-import-export`). **Depends on:** 07 (brand), 08 (i18n), 01. **Schema/RLS/auth/permission/flag impact:** NONE — no DB, no migration, no RLS, no new permission or flag. Isolation ➖. The screenshot bypass is env-gated (staging-only), fail-closed.

**Problem.** Every later screen must be modern, polished, and usable by non-technical/illiterate users AND meet a hard 90+ mobile performance budget — with no shared design system, modules would drift into inconsistent, slow, raw HTML. This step lands the shared `@mp/ui` system + the performance/Lighthouse gate + the staging screenshot bypass.

**What changed.**

*Package `@mp/ui` (scaffold → full React design system).* Was a pure-helper scaffold (`cn`, `themeCssVars`); now a Tailwind + shadcn/ui-style component library.
- **Toolchain:** React 19 peer dep; deps `@radix-ui/react-{dialog,label,popover,slot,tabs}`, `class-variance-authority`, `clsx`, `tailwind-merge`, `lucide-react`, `recharts`; dev `tailwindcss`, `jest`+`jest-environment-jsdom`+`@testing-library/{react,jest-dom,user-event}`. tsconfig → `module esnext` / `moduleResolution bundler` / `lib DOM` / `jsx react-jsx`. jsdom jest config with `jest.setup.ts` (matchMedia + ResizeObserver stubs).
- **Theming:** `cn` upgraded (clsx+twMerge). `tailwind-preset.ts` (`@mp/ui/tailwind-preset`) maps `--brand-*` → semantic Tailwind tokens (`primary/accent/destructive` follow the tenant palette; `background/card/muted/border` are light/dark `--mp-*`), plus `min-h-touch` (44px), brand fonts, motion keyframes. `styles.css` layers `@tailwind` + the `--mp-*` light/dark token layer (derived from brand) + reduced-motion guard. `theme.tsx` `ThemeProvider`/`useTheme` — light/dark/system, class-based (`.dark` on `<html>`), persisted, follows OS in `system`.
- **Components:** Button (cva variants, large-touch, `asChild`), Input/Textarea, Label, Card(+parts), Badge, Skeleton/SkeletonText (shimmer), Spinner, Field (a11y label+hint+error wiring), EmptyState, Dialog(+`Modal` alias, focus-trap), Toast (`ToastProvider`/`useToast`/`Toaster`, aria-live), SearchSelect + MultiSearchSelect (Radix Popover combobox, filter, large-touch), DateField, Tabs, **ModuleTabs** (ACTIVE-ONLY mount — inactive tabs' `render()` NOT called until first opened → lazy per-tab fetch; `unmountInactive` opt), **DataList** (client search + pagination + toolbar slot + `onExport(filteredRows)`→12, skeleton rows, empty state, a11y caption), animated recharts **Chart** wrappers (Line/Area/Bar/Donut, brand-ramp colours, dynamic-import friendly), **AppShell** (brand header + sidebar; `visibleNav` filters by injected `hasFlag`/`can` predicates so a disabled module/absent permission → NO nav entry; slots for language/theme/account), Feature (prop-driven flag wrapper), ShortcutScope (`mod+k`/sequence combos, suppressed in inputs unless opted in, `eventToToken`), VoiceInput/`useVoiceInput` (Web Speech, locale-aware, self-hides when unsupported).
- **Pure testable seams:** `screenshotBypassEnabled`/`screenshotTokenValid`/`grantsScreenshotAccess` (+ `SCREENSHOT_TOKEN_PARAM`), exposed on the lean **`@mp/ui/screenshot`** subpath so the edge middleware imports the logic WITHOUT dragging React/Radix in. `evaluateBudgets`/`withinBudget`/`DEFAULT_BUDGETS` perf-budget model (longest-prefix route match, JS+total ceilings).

*Web app wiring.* `tailwind.config.ts` spreads the `@mp/ui` preset + scans app & `packages/ui/src`; `postcss.config.mjs` (tailwind+autoprefixer); `globals.css` gains the `@tailwind` layers + `--mp-*` tokens at the TOP (legacy `.mp-*` styles kept below, authoritative on conflict); `ThemeProvider` added to `layout.tsx` (`defaultMode="system"`); added dep `lucide-react`. **`/ui` showcase** (server shell + `UiShowcase` client) built ENTIRELY from @mp/ui, framed in AppShell (nav proves Pharmacy-POS flag OFF → hidden, Lab ON → shown), dynamic-imported chart (`DemoChart` via `next/dynamic ssr:false`), all copy from new `ui.*` i18n keys → polished light/dark, RTL in Urdu, brand-token driven. **`middleware.ts`** screenshot token (matcher excludes static assets). **`/lh-bloated`** intentional canary (`import * as` lucide + eager chart → 431 kB first-load vs `/ui` 279 kB).

*Perf / Lighthouse gate.* `lighthouserc.json` (LHCI: `next start`, public routes `/ /login /ui`, mobile emulation, assert perf/a11y/best-practices `minScore 0.9`, `budgetsPath`) + `budgets.json` (script 250 KB / total 700 KB / timing budgets). `.github/workflows/ci.yml`: the Lighthouse **stub replaced** with a real job (build web + deps → `lhci autorun`) + a NEGATIVE step that fails if `/lh-bloated` scores ≥90 (proves the gate bites). Root `lighthouse` script. The internal "fast-&-smooth" budget check is the unit-tested `evaluateBudgets` seam (a 900-KiB route fails).

**i18n keys.** New nested `ui.*` block (58 keys) added to EN + UR catalogs (parity preserved) covering the showcase, nav labels, theme-toggle labels, and the demo tag.

**Runtime verification (driven via `next start`).**
- Screenshot token — Case A (NODE_ENV=production, APP_ENV unset): `/ui` 200; `/ui?screenshot_token=<secret>` **200 with NO `x-mp-screenshot` header** (bypass OFF regardless, param ignored, fail-closed). Case B (APP_ENV=staging): correct token → **200 + `x-mp-screenshot: read-only`**; wrong token → **403**.
- `/ui` SSR HTML contains design-system utilities (`min-h-touch`, `bg-primary`/`text-brand`), a compiled `/_next/static/css/*` stylesheet, the showcase heading, and the AppShell nav with Lab shown + Pharmacy-POS hidden (flag-gated).

**Do-NOT-break honoured.** 07 brand `--brand-*` contract + 08 i18n unchanged; @mp/ui component APIs are additive/stable; Lighthouse gate + budgets now permanent in CI; screenshot bypass fail-closed & staging-only.

**Verification gates (all green).** typecheck **26/26**; lint **15/15**; turbo build **15/15** (web build: `/ui` 279 kB / `/lh-bloated` 431 kB first-load, middleware 34.5 kB); jest **19 tasks** — NEW `@mp/ui` **38/38** (8 suites: cn, screenshot, perf-budget, button, data-list, module-tabs, app-shell, misc[theme/feature/shortcut/toast/search-select]) + api 175/175 + import 18/18 + db 67/67 + notifications 18/18 + offline 29/29 + consent 18/18 + **i18n 19/19 incl. EN↔UR parity**. White-label: brand-token driven (verified); RTL verified. Performance: Lighthouse job wired in CI (not run in-sandbox — no Chrome); budget logic unit-proven.

**Notes / caveats.**
- Lighthouse itself is CI-only (needs headless Chrome, not available in this sandbox); the config + budgets + negative canary are committed and the budget-evaluation logic is unit-tested here.
- `MODULE_TYPELESS_PACKAGE_JSON` warning on `dist/tailwind-preset.js` when Next loads the config is cosmetic; `@mp/ui` is NOT marked `type:module` on purpose (its CJS `jest.config.js`/`jest.setup.ts` would break).
- Urdu font strategy stays the 08 local-font stack; a self-hosted subset woff2 (same `unicode-range`+`font-display:swap` contract) is `[DECIDE AT BUILD]` if local fonts prove insufficient.

## Build-step 12 — Foundation: Import / Export Engine

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase:** Foundation / item 12. **Branch:** `feat/12-import-export` (stacked on `feat/11-consent-terms`). **Depends on:** 02 (tenancy/RLS), 04 (RBAC permission), 06 (audit). **Reused by:** 14 patients, 19 lab catalog, 20/28 pharmacy, 29 suppliers — generic engine.
- **Schema/migration/RLS/permission impact:** NEW migration `20260704090000_import_export` — two tenant-scoped tables + one enum (`CREATE TYPE "ImportStatus"`). Both tables call the canonical `apply_tenant_rls()` (02) → `tenant_isolation` policy (visible/writable only under own `app.tenant_id` GUC; WITH CHECK blocks cross-tenant writes; no-context → zero rows, fail-closed). NO new permission — the sample importer reuses the existing `purchase.manage` (suppliers). NO new global guard (routes ride the JwtAuthGuard; per-entity permission checked programmatically). No auth-contract change; no feature flag (import/export is always-on infra).

**Problem.** A tenant onboards by loading 20k–50k medicines, a test catalog, patients and suppliers from Excel/CSV, and must export anything it can see. Hand entry is impossible; a bad import is dangerous. Need validated, previewable, resumable bulk import + universal filtered export, idempotent by natural key (no duplicates on re-import).

**What changed.**
- **NEW pure package `@mp/import`** (framework-free, side-effect-free, deterministic — reused by API + web + every consuming module):
  - the `Importer<Parsed>` contract each module declares: `entity`, `permission`, `columns` (`ColumnSpec{key,header,type,required,example}`), `upsertKey` (natural key), `validateRow(coerced,rowNumber)`, `transformRow(coerced)`;
  - an **RFC-4180 CSV/TSV codec**: `parseDelimited`/`parseCsv` (quoted fields, `""` escapes, embedded commas/newlines, CRLF or LF, unquoted-cell trim, blank-line skip, case-insensitive header match) + `serializeDelimited`/`serializeCsv` (quote only where required, stringify non-string/null);
  - `buildTemplate` (header + one example row); `dryRun` (structural required/type coercion → then importer `validateRow` only on clean rows → valid/invalid split + transformed `validRows` + `errors[]` + `missingHeaders`, NOTHING persisted); `buildErrorReportCsv` (row/field/message); `planUpsert` (collapse by natural key, last-wins, trimmed+case-insensitive key → no duplicates) + `chunk`; `ImportStatus`/`IMPORT_STATUSES` vocabulary.
- **DB:** `ImportJob` (`status ImportStatus` default VALIDATED, `total`/`valid`/`invalid`/`applied` progress counters, `payload Json?` = staged transformed valid rows for apply, `errorReport String?` = inline CSV, `errorReportKey String?` RESERVED for future R2 object key, `createdBy`, `@@index([tenantId,entity])`) + `ImportStatus` enum (`UPLOADED|VALIDATED|APPLYING|DONE|FAILED`) + demo target `ImportDemoSupplier` (`name`/`phone`/`city`, `@@unique([tenantId,phone])`). `ImportStatus` re-exported from `@mp/db`. Isolation proven in `packages/db/src/import-isolation.spec.ts` (real 01→12 migrations in pglite; T1/T2 see only own jobs+rows, WITH CHECK blocks cross-tenant insert, no-context → 0 rows).
- **API `ImportModule`:** `ImportRegistry` (maps entity→`EntityImporter` = pure spec + `upsertChunk(tenantId,rows)` + `exportColumns` + `exportRows(tenantId,filters)`; ships sample `demoSupplierImporter` bound to the demo target, natural key `phone`, `validateRow` enforces 7–15 digit phone). `ImportService`: `upload` (parse → dryRun → create VALIDATED job staging validRows + errorReport; returns preview counts + first 100 errors + errorCount, writes NOTHING to target) · `apply` (planUpsert dedupe → APPLYING → chunked (`APPLY_CHUNK_SIZE=500`) idempotent `upsertChunk`, `setApplied` per chunk for progress, resume from `applied` offset, on error → FAILED keeping progress, else → DONE; re-applying a DONE job is a no-op) · `getTemplate` · `getJob`/`listJobs` · `getErrorReport` · `exportCsv` (importer `exportRows` honours filters, serialized to CSV). Repo seam `ImportRepo` + `PrismaImportRepo` (Prisma `upsert` by compound unique `tenantId_phone`) + `FakeImportRepo`. Controller (`@Controller()`): `GET /import/:entity/template`, `POST /import/:entity/upload` (`@Audited import.upload`), `POST /import/:entity/:jobId/apply` (`@Audited import.apply`), `GET /import/:entity/jobs`, `GET /import/:entity/:jobId`, `GET /import/:entity/:jobId/errors`, `GET /export/:listKey?filters` — each resolves the entity's importer (404 if unknown) and checks its DYNAMIC permission via `PermissionService.roleHasPermission` (403 if missing); CSV endpoints set `Content-Type: text/csv`. `ImportModule` imports `PermissionsModule`, exports `ImportRegistry`+`ImportService`; registered last in `AppModule` (no global guard → order immaterial).
- **Web (EN+UR):** `/admin/import` server shell + `ImportWizard` client island — entity picker (demo_supplier), step 1 download template, step 2 paste/upload CSV → Validate → PREVIEW (total/valid/invalid chips, missing-header warning, row-error table + "…N more" + error-report download), step 3 confirm apply (disabled when 0 valid) → applied summary / failed-retry hint, plus a filtered Export (city filter) button. Access probed on mount (401→sign-in, 403→no-access). CSV downloads via fetch+Blob. New `mp-import-*` styles in `globals.css`; 34 EN+UR i18n keys (parity green).
- **Launch notes ([DECIDE AT BUILD]):** upload takes CSV/TSV text as a JSON field today (multipart/streamed upload via a FileInterceptor deferred); `payload` staged as an inline JSON blob + apply runs in-process chunked (object/blob store for large payloads + Redis/worker background dispatch deferred; `errorReportKey` reserved for R2 offload); the engine is codec-agnostic — Excel/xlsx (SheetJS) parse/serialize is a swappable codec deferred (CSV/TSV shipped).
- **Verification gates (all green):** typecheck **26/26**, lint **15/15**, turbo build **15/15**; jest — `@mp/import` **18/18** (codec/template/dryRun/error-report/planUpsert/chunk), `@mp/db` **67/67** (11 suites; +6 import-isolation), `@mp/api` **175/175** (22 suites; +11 import e2e incl. 401/403/404 gating, dry-run-writes-nothing, apply-idempotent-no-duplicate, audited, error-report, filtered export, 20k-row background apply with progress, FAILED-job resume), `@mp/i18n` **19/19** (incl. EN↔UR parity), unchanged: notifications 18/18, offline 29/29, consent 18/18. Isolation: import jobs + imported rows tenant-scoped (T1/T2 pglite proof). No feature-flag/vertical/performance/white-label surface at this step.

## Build-step 11 — Foundation: Terms & Consent Gate

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase:** Foundation / item 11. **Branch:** `feat/11-consent-terms` (stacked on `feat/10-offline-core`). **Depends on:** 02 (tenancy/RLS), 03 (auth principal), 06 (audit).
- **Schema/migration/RLS/permission impact:** NEW migration `20260703180000_consent_terms` — two tenant-scoped tables + three enums. Both tables call the canonical `apply_tenant_rls()` (02) → `tenant_isolation` policy (visible/writable only under own `app.tenant_id` GUC; WITH CHECK blocks cross-tenant writes; no-context → zero rows, fail-closed). NEW tenant permission `consent.manage` (added to `PERMISSIONS` + `ADMIN` role defaults in `@mp/shared`). NEW global `ConsentGuard` registered by `ConsentModule` (acts only on `@RequiresConsent` routes; runs after `JwtAuthGuard`). No auth-contract change; no feature flag (consent is always-on infra).

**Problem.** Liability protection needs explicit, VERSIONED, logged consent — staff (system use), patients (treatment, data use, AI disclaimer), tenants (service terms). The AI assistant must capture a disclaimer before first use. Wording changes after a Pakistani-lawyer review → it must be DATA, not code, and a new version must re-prompt.

**What changed.**
- **NEW pure package `@mp/consent`** (framework-free, side-effect-free, deterministic — caller passes `nowMs`; reused by web + API + unit tests):
  - Vocabulary: `ConsentAudience` (STAFF/PATIENT/TENANT), `ConsentType` (SYSTEM_USE/TREATMENT/DATA_USE/AI_ASSISTANT_DISCLAIMER/SERVICE_TERMS), `ConsentSubjectType` (USER/PATIENT), `ConsentLang` (EN/UR); ordered `CONSENT_*` arrays; `AUDIENCE_SUBJECT` map.
  - `REQUIRED_CONSENTS` — the blanket onboarding gate per audience (STAFF→[SYSTEM_USE], PATIENT→[TREATMENT,DATA_USE], TENANT→[SERVICE_TERMS]). `AI_ASSISTANT_DISCLAIMER` deliberately NOT blanket — it is an ACTION gate via `@RequiresConsent`.
  - `effectiveDocument` / `effectiveDocumentsByType` — the CURRENT version = newest whose `effectiveFrom` has passed (future-dated publish does not prompt yet), language-preferred.
  - `isConsentSatisfied` / `outstandingConsents` / `gateFor` — the gate: a subject satisfies a type iff it holds a record at version ≥ current; a NEW (higher) version re-opens the gate; older records stay valid history. A required type with no in-force document is omitted (enforceable the moment one is published, no code change).
  - `sanitizeConsentContext` + `maskIp` — whitelist only safe keys (`ip`/`userAgent`/`source`/`lang`), mask the IP (v4 last octet→`x`, v6 keep 2 hextets), clamp lengths, drop unknown keys, return `undefined` when nothing safe remains (§5 — no raw sensitive data ever stored).
  - 18 unit tests (`consent.spec.ts`).
- **DB (`@mp/db`):** `ConsentDocument` (id, tenantId, audience, type, lang, version, title, body=SWAPPABLE legal text, effectiveFrom, supersedesId, updatedBy, createdAt; `@@unique([tenantId,audience,type,lang,version])`, `@@index([tenantId,audience,type])`) + `ConsentRecord` (id, tenantId, subjectType, subjectId, documentId, type, version, context Json?, acceptedAt; `@@index([tenantId,subjectType,subjectId])`, `@@index([tenantId,documentId])`) + enums `Audience`/`ConsentType`/`SubjectType`. NEW `consent-isolation.spec.ts` (pglite, real 01–11 migrations): T1 sees only its own docs/records, wording never bleeds, WITH CHECK blocks cross-tenant publish + accept, no-context → zero rows.
- **API (`ConsentModule`):** `ConsentService` over a `ConsentRepo` seam (`PrismaConsentRepo` via `runWithTenant`; `FakeConsentRepo` for e2e) + injectable `CONSENT_CLOCK`. `publishDocument()` (auto-increment version, link `supersedesId`, default effective=now — editing wording = new version = re-open gate, no redeploy), `required()` (outstanding docs for an audience), `accept()` (idempotent per subject+type+version; masked context), `isTypeSatisfied()` (fail-closed; backs the guard). Global `ConsentGuard` + `@RequiresConsent(type)` decorator → 403 `{ error:'consent_required', type, document, message }` until current version accepted — the STABLE contract AI steps (32/36–39) reuse. Endpoints `/consent`: `GET documents` + `PUT documents` (gated by `consent.manage`, `@Audited consent.document.publish`), `GET required?audience=&lang=` + `POST accept` (any-authed, tenant-scoped, `@Audited consent.accept`, context masked from req ip/user-agent), `GET demo/ai` (`@RequiresConsent('AI_ASSISTANT_DISCLAIMER')` — proves the gate). 10 e2e tests (`consent.e2e.spec.ts`).
- **Web:** EN+UR `/admin/consent` (`ConsentManager` island) — publish a versioned doc per audience/type/lang with live direction-aware (UR RTL) preview, optional effective date, and the published-versions list; server enforces `consent.manage`. EN+UR `/consent` (`ConsentGate` island) — the outstanding STAFF documents, each readable + scrollable, an EN/UR document-language toggle that re-fetches, scroll-to-end-then-explicit-"I agree" recording the exact version. 37 NEW i18n keys added to BOTH catalogs (parity kept). Consent-specific CSS in `globals.css`.
- **Enum labels:** consent types/audiences rendered via `consentType*`/`consentAudience*` catalog keys (no raw codes).

**Launch note / `[DECIDE AT BUILD]`:** final legal wording is a Pakistani lawyer's call — the model keeps it swappable as `ConsentDocument.body` via an admin edit, no code change. Patient/tenant subject wiring (14/31) plugs the patient subject through `ConsentService` directly; the `@RequiresConsent` + `AI_ASSISTANT_DISCLAIMER` contract is stable.

**Fixes during integration (pre-commit, uncommitted WIP was mid-flight):** (1) e2e `OTP_TRANSPORT` override used `{ deliver }` — corrected to the real `OtpTransport.send` interface (09 swapped the transport). (2) the AI-demo e2e asserted `body.message.error`/`.type`; NestJS serializes a `ForbiddenException(object)` payload as the body verbatim, so corrected to `body.error`/`body.type` (matches the guard's deliberate structured payload).

**Verification gates (all green):** typecheck 24/24 · lint 14/14 · turbo build 14/14 (both `/admin/consent` + `/consent` routes emitted) · jest: `@mp/db` 61/61 (10 suites, incl. consent-isolation T1/T2), `@mp/api` 164/164 (21 suites, incl. 10 consent e2e), `@mp/i18n` 19/19 (incl. EN↔UR parity, +37 keys), `@mp/consent` 18/18, `@mp/notifications` 18/18, `@mp/offline` 29/29 · i18n parity: EQUAL · isolation: T1/T2 proven (documents + records + WITH CHECK + fail-closed).
- **Files:** NEW `packages/consent/**` (pkg + `src/index.ts` + `src/consent.spec.ts` + configs), `packages/db/prisma/migrations/20260703180000_consent_terms/migration.sql`, `packages/db/src/consent-isolation.spec.ts`, `apps/api/src/consent/**` (module, service, controller, guard, repositories, dto, constants, __fakes__, index, e2e), `apps/web/app/admin/consent/{page.tsx,ConsentManager.tsx}`, `apps/web/app/consent/{page.tsx,ConsentGate.tsx}`. MODIFIED `packages/db/prisma/schema.prisma` (2 models + 3 enums), `packages/shared/src/permissions.ts` (`consent.manage`), `apps/api/src/app.module.ts` (import `ConsentModule`), `apps/api/package.json` + `pnpm-lock.yaml` (`@mp/consent` dep), `packages/i18n/src/messages/{en,ur}.json` (+37 keys), `apps/web/app/globals.css` (consent styles).
